__fastcall TFormChart::TFormChart( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;T<a href="CppComponent.htm">Component</a>* Owner, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt;&amp; losses, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt;&amp; wins) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;: TForm(Owner), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanClose(<b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b>) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(losses.size() <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> wins.size() ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt; losses<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>(losses.size()); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt; wins<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>(wins.size()); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppCopy.htm">std::copy</a>(losses.begin(), losses.end(), losses<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>.begin()); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppCopy.htm">std::copy</a>(wins.begin(), wins.end(), wins<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>.begin()); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;Chart1-&gt;Series[0]-&gt;<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a>Array( &amp;(losses<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>[0]), losses<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>.size() <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 1); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;Chart1-&gt;Series[1]-&gt;<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a>Array( &amp;(wins<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>[0]), wins<a href="CppDouble.htm">Double</a>.size() <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 1); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormChart::<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r1<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanClose <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>; <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormChart::ButtonCloseClick(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mCanClose <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) Close(); <br/>
} <br/>

<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
__fastcall TFormClassicTronGame::TFormClassicTronGame( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;T<a href="CppComponent.htm">Component</a>* Owner, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;&amp; players, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> speed, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxx, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxy, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppBool.htm">bool</a></b> donut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppBool.htm">bool</a></b> canWalkThroughOwnColor) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;: TForm(Owner), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers(players), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mMaxx(maxx), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mMaxy(maxy), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld(donut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanWalkThroughOwnColor(canWalkThroughOwnColor) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;Constraints-&gt;MinWidth&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> maxx <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (Width <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> ClientWidth); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;Constraints-&gt;MinHeight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> maxy <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (Height <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> ClientHeight); <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Put the players on screen in the correct position <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> nPlayers <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.size(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>nPlayers; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(nPlayers); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> angle <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (0.5 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ( fraction * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a> * 2.0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].x <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxx) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 2.0) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppSin.htm">std::sin</a>( angle ) * 10.0 ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].y <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxx) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 2.0) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ( <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a><a href="CppCos.htm">std::cos</a>( angle ) * 10.0 ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (angle &lt; 0.75 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) mPlayers[i].direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (angle &lt; 1.25 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) mPlayers[i].direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 2; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (angle &lt; 1.75 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) mPlayers[i].direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 3; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (angle &lt; 2.25 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) mPlayers[i].direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 0; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (angle &lt; 2.75 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) mPlayers[i].direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;Interval <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> speed; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic-&gt;Width&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic-&gt;Height <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppPaint.htm">Paint</a>Vcl(ImageBuffer,clBlack); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;On<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r(0); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronGame::FormKeyDown(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WORD &amp;Key, TShift<a href="CppState.htm">State</a> Shift) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;keyLeft&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key) { i-&gt;direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (i-&gt;direction <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> 3) <a href="CppOperatorModulus.htm">%</a> 4; } <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;keyRight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key) { i-&gt;direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (i-&gt;direction <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> 1) <a href="CppOperatorModulus.htm">%</a> 4; } <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key; <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronGame::<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Check <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> collisions <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> xTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).x; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> yTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).y; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppSwitch.htm">switch</a></b> ((*i).direction) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 0: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Up <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;yTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).y <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> yTo &lt; 0) yTo<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 1: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Right <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;xTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).x <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> xTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxx) xTo<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 2: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Down <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;yTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).y <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> yTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxy) yTo<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 3: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Left <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;xTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (*i).x <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 1; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> xTo &lt; 0) xTo<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b> <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> ( xTo &lt; 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> yTo &lt; 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> xTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxx <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> yTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxy) ) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(*i).direction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> ((*i).direction <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> 2) <a href="CppOperatorModulus.htm">%</a> 4; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppContinue.htm">continue</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <a href="CppGetPixel.htm">GetPixel</a>Vcl(ImageBuffer, xTo, yTo); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> clBlack <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;TColor&gt;(-1) ) <b><a href="CppContinue.htm">continue</a></b>; <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Nothing there... <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (color<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>(*i).color) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a><a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>ToWinners(color); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> color<a href="CppOperatorEqual.htm">==</a>(*i).color) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Move the players <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppSwitch.htm">switch</a></b> ((*i).direction) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 0: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Up <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a>-(*i).y; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> ((*i).y &lt; 0) (*i).y<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 1: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Right <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(*i).x; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> ((*i).x <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxx) (*i).x<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 2: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Down <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(*i).y; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> ((*i).y <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxy) (*i).y<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 3: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Left <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a>-(*i).x; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> ((*i).x &lt; 0) (*i).x<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Draw <b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> player locations to buffer <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SetPixel(ImageBuffer, (*i).x, (*i).y, (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Draw buffer to screen <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;Canvas-&gt;StretchDraw(<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;ClientRect,ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> TFormClassicTronGame::<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a><a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>ToWinners(<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> color) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(i-&gt;nWins); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> TFormClassicTronGame::Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers(<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> color) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(i-&gt;nLose); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronGame::FormClose(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TCloseAction &amp;Action) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;Enabled <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> size <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.size(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt; losses(size); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt; wins(size); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>size; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;losses[i] <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers[i].nLose; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;wins[i]&nbsp;&nbsp; <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers[i].nWins; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormChart&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormChart(0,losses,wins)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
} <br/>

<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronMenu::ButtonCalibrateClick(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> nPlayers <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> PanelNplayers-&gt;Caption.<a href="CppToInt.htm">ToInt</a>Def(-1); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(nPlayers<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>-1); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers.resize(nPlayers); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>nPlayers; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Key left <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> String message <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Player #" <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> <a href="CppIntToStr.htm">IntToStr</a>(i+1) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ", please press key <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> 'Turn left'."; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormPressKey&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormPressKey(0,message)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].keyLeft <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Key right <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> String message <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Player #" <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> <a href="CppIntToStr.htm">IntToStr</a>(i+1) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ", please press key <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> 'Turn right'."; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormPressKey&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormPressKey(0,message)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].keyRight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Color <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Choose color <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormSelectColor&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormSelectColor(0)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> colorIndex <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 10; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(colorIndex <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> colorIndex &lt; 20); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(colorIndex) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 20.0; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppUnsigned.htm">unsigned</a></b> <b><a href="CppChar.htm">char</a></b> r,g,b; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppRainbow.htm">Rainbow</a>(fraction,r,g,b); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> RgbToColor(r,g,b); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ButtonStart-&gt;Enabled <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>; <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronMenu::ButtonStartClick(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionSpeed <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionWidth <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarWidth-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarWidth-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionHeight <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarHeight-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarHeight-&gt;Max); <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> speed <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 1000.0 <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> (fractionSpeed * 999.0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(speed &gt; 0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxx <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 100.0 <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (fractionWidth * <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(Monitor-&gt;Width <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 200)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxy <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 100.0 <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (fractionHeight * <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(Monitor-&gt;Height <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 200)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormClassicTronGame&gt; f( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormClassicTronGame( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;speed, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;maxx, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;maxy, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronMenu::FormKeyDown(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WORD &amp;Key, TShift<a href="CppState.htm">State</a> Shift) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppSwitch.htm">switch</a></b>(Key) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> VK_ADD: <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageNplayersPlus-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> VK_SUBTRACT: <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageNplayersMinus-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 83: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a> 's' <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageWorldFlat-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageWorldDonut-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 72: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a> 'h' <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageCannotWalkThroughOwnColor-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageCanWalkThroughOwnColor-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>

<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormClassicTronMenu::TrackBarSpeedChange(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.1) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Slowest"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.40) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Slow"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.60) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Normal"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.90) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Fast"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Fastest"; <br/>
} <br/>

<a href="CppInclude.htm">#include</a> &lt;<a href="CppMemoryH.htm">memory</a>&gt; <br/>

<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
__fastcall TFormSuperTronGame::TFormSuperTronGame( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;T<a href="CppComponent.htm">Component</a>* Owner, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;&amp; players, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> speed, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxx, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxy, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppBool.htm">bool</a></b> donut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppBool.htm">bool</a></b> canWalkThroughOwnColor) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;: TForm(Owner), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers(players), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mMaxx(maxx), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mMaxy(maxy), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld(donut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld), <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanWalkThroughOwnColor(canWalkThroughOwnColor) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;Constraints-&gt;MinWidth&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> maxx <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (Width <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> ClientWidth); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;Constraints-&gt;MinHeight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> maxy <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (Height <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> ClientHeight); <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Put the players on screen in the correct position <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> nPlayers <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.size(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>nPlayers; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(nPlayers); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> angle <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (0.5 * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ( fraction * <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a> * 2.0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].x <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxx) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 2.0) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppSin.htm">std::sin</a>( angle ) * 10.0 ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].y <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> (<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxx) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 2.0) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ( <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a><a href="CppCos.htm">std::cos</a>( angle ) * 10.0 ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].angle <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> angle; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;Interval <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> speed; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic-&gt;Width&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic-&gt;Height <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppPaint.htm">Paint</a>Vcl(ImageBuffer,clBlack); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;On<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r(0); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronGame::FormKeyDown(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WORD &amp;Key, TShift<a href="CppState.htm">State</a> Shift) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;keyLeft&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key) { i-&gt;angle <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> SuperTronPlayer::deltaAngle; } <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;keyRight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key) { i-&gt;angle <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> SuperTronPlayer::deltaAngle; } <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> Key; <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronGame::<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>r(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Check <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> collisions <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> xFrom <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i-&gt;x); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> yFrom <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i-&gt;y); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> xTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt;(<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i-&gt;x) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (<a href="CppSin.htm">std::sin</a>(i-&gt;angle) * Player::speed)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> yTo <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt;(<b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(i-&gt;y) <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> (<a href="CppCos.htm">std::cos</a>(i-&gt;angle) * Player::speed)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (xTo &lt;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0) xTo<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (xTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxx) xTo<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (yTo &lt;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0) yTo<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (yTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxy) yTo<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>mMaxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> ( xTo &lt; 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> yTo &lt; 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> xTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxx <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> yTo <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> mMaxy ) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(*i).angle <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <a href="CppM_PI.htm">M_PI</a>; <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Reverse direction <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppContinue.htm">continue</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (xFrom <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> xTo <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> yFrom <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> yTo) <b><a href="CppContinue.htm">continue</a></b>; <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>No movement visible <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <a href="CppGetPixel.htm">GetPixel</a>Vcl(ImageBuffer, xTo, yTo); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> clBlack <a href="CppOperatorLogicalOr.htm">||</a> color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;TColor&gt;(-1) ) <b><a href="CppContinue.htm">continue</a></b>; <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Nothing there... <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (color<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>(*i).color) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a><a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>ToWinners(color); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b> <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> color<a href="CppOperatorEqual.htm">==</a>(*i).color) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers( (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RemoveColor(ImageBuffer, color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Move the players <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> maxx <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxx); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> maxy <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(mMaxy); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i-&gt;x<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>(<a href="CppSin.htm">std::sin</a>(i-&gt;angle) * Player::speed); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i-&gt;y<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>(<a href="CppCos.htm">std::cos</a>(i-&gt;angle) * Player::speed); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;x &lt;&nbsp;&nbsp; 0.0) i-&gt;x<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>maxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;x <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> maxx) i-&gt;x<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>maxx; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;y &lt;&nbsp;&nbsp; 0.0) i-&gt;y<a href="CppOperatorPlusAssign.htm">+=</a>maxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;y <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> maxy) i-&gt;y<a href="CppOperatorMinusAssign.htm">-=</a>maxy; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Draw <b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> player locations to buffer <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SetPixel(ImageBuffer, (*i).x, (*i).y, (*i).color ); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Draw buffer to screen <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;Canvas-&gt;StretchDraw(<b><a href="CppThis.htm">this</a></b>-&gt;ClientRect,ImageBuffer-&gt;Picture-&gt;Graphic); <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> TFormSuperTronGame::<a href="CppAdd.htm">Add</a><a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>ToWinners(<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> color) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(i-&gt;nWins); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> TFormSuperTronGame::Remove<a href="CppPoint.htm">Point</a>FromLosers(<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> TColor color) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> j <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.end(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;Player&gt;::<a href="CppIterator.htm">iterator</a> i <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.begin(); i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>j; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (i-&gt;color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> color) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+(i-&gt;nLose); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>
<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>--------------------------------------------------------------------------- <br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronGame::FormClose(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TCloseAction &amp;Action) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppTime.htm">Time</a>rGame-&gt;Enabled <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppFalse.htm">false</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> size <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers.size(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt; losses(size); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppVector.htm">std::vector</a>&lt;<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b>&gt; wins(size); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>size; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;losses[i] <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers[i].nLose; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;wins[i]&nbsp;&nbsp; <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> mPlayers[i].nWins; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormChart&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormChart(0,losses,wins)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
} <br/>

<br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronMenu::ButtonCalibrateClick(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> nPlayers <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> PanelNplayers-&gt;Caption.<a href="CppToInt.htm">ToInt</a>Def(-1); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(nPlayers<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>-1); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers.resize(nPlayers); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> (<b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> i=0; i<a href="CppOperatorNotEqual.htm">!=</a>nPlayers; <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a>+i) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Key left <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> String message <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Player #" <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> <a href="CppIntToStr.htm">IntToStr</a>(i+1) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ", please press key <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> 'Turn left'."; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormPressKey&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormPressKey(0,message)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].keyLeft <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Key right <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> String message <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Player #" <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> <a href="CppIntToStr.htm">IntToStr</a>(i+1) <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> ", please press key <b><a href="CppFor.htm">for</a></b> 'Turn right'."; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormPressKey&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormPressKey(0,message)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].keyRight <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Color <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppComment.htm">//</a>Choose color <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAuto_ptr.htm">std::auto_ptr</a>&lt;TFormSelectColor&gt; f(<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormSelectColor(0)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> colorIndex <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> f-&gt;ModalResult <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 10; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(colorIndex <a href="CppOperatorGreaterEqual.htm">&gt;=</a> 0 <a href="CppOperatorLogicalAnd.htm">&amp;&amp;</a> colorIndex &lt; 20); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(colorIndex) <a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> 20.0; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppUnsigned.htm">unsigned</a></b> <b><a href="CppChar.htm">char</a></b> r,g,b; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppRainbow.htm">Rainbow</a>(fraction,r,g,b); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers[i].color <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> RgbToColor(r,g,b); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;ButtonStart-&gt;Enabled <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>; <br/>
} <br/>

<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronMenu::ButtonStartClick(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionSpeed <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionWidth <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarWidth-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarWidth-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fractionHeight <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarHeight-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarHeight-&gt;Max); <br/>
<br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> speed <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 1000.0 <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> (fractionSpeed * 999.0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppAssert.htm">assert</a>(speed &gt; 0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxx <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 100.0 <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (fractionWidth * <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(Monitor-&gt;Width <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 200)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppInt.htm">int</a></b> maxy <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> 100.0 <a href="CppOperatorPlus.htm">+</a> (fractionHeight * <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(Monitor-&gt;Height <a href="CppOperatorMinus.htm">-</a> 200)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppScoped_ptr.htm">boost::scoped_ptr</a>&lt;TFormSuperTronGame&gt; f( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppNew.htm">new</a></b> TFormSuperTronGame( <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mPlayers, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;speed, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;maxx, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;maxy, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;f-&gt;ShowModal(); <br/>
} <br/>

<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronMenu::FormKeyDown(TObject *Sender, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WORD &amp;Key, TShift<a href="CppState.htm">State</a> Shift) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppSwitch.htm">switch</a></b>(Key) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> VK_ADD: <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageNplayersPlus-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> VK_SUBTRACT: <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageNplayersMinus-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 83: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a> 's' <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mDonut<a href="CppShape.htm">Shape</a>dWorld <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageWorldFlat-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageWorldDonut-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppCase.htm">case</a></b> 72: <a href="CppComment.htm">//</a> 'h' <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (mCanWalkThroughOwnColor <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a><a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppTrue.htm">true</a></b>) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageCannotWalkThroughOwnColor-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ImageCanWalkThroughOwnColor-&gt;OnClick(0); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppBreak.htm">break</a></b>; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;} <br/>
} <br/>

<br/>
<b><a href="CppVoid.htm">void</a></b> __fastcall TFormSuperTronMenu::TrackBarSpeedChange(TObject *Sender) <br/>
{ <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b> fraction <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Position) <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="CppOperatorDivide.htm">/</a> <b><a href="CppStatic_cast.htm">static_cast</a></b>&lt;<b><a href="CppDouble.htm">double</a></b>&gt;(TrackBarSpeed-&gt;Max); <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.1) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Slowest"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.40) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Slow"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.60) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Normal"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> <b><a href="CppIf.htm">if</a></b> (fraction &lt; 0.90) PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Fast"; <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppElse.htm">else</a></b> PanelSpeedValue-&gt;Caption <a href="CppOperatorAssign.htm">=</a> "Fastest"; <br/>
} <br/>

&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppUnsigned.htm">unsigned</a></b> <b><a href="CppChar.htm">char</a></b> red, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppUnsigned.htm">unsigned</a></b> <b><a href="CppChar.htm">char</a></b> green, <br/>
&nbsp;&nbsp;<b><a href="CppConst.htm">const</a></b> <b><a href="CppUnsigned.htm">unsigned</a></b> <b><a href="CppChar.htm">char</a></b> blue&nbsp;&nbsp;); <br/>
<br/>
<br/>
<br/>
<a href="CppEndif.htm">#endif</a> <br/>
</code></td></tr></table>
